  // Auto pagination
  $(function() {
    $('#problem_list_pagination').AutoPagination({
      nextPageSelector: 'a.nextPage',
      panelSelector: 'a.problem-panel',

<script>
  function get_filter_data_json() {
    var options = $('.filter-label');
    var tag_list = []
    var status_list = []
    var difficulty_list = []

    for (var i = 0; i < options.length; ++i) {
      var dataValue = options[i].getAttribute('data-value');
      if (options[i].getAttribute('category') == 'tag')
        tag_list.push(dataValue);
      else if (options[i].getAttribute('category') == 'status')
        status_list.push(dataValue);
      else if (options[i].getAttribute('category') == 'difficulty')
        difficulty_list.push(dataValue);
    }
    var filter_data = {
      'tags': tag_list,
      'status': status_list,
      'difficulty': difficulty_list
    }
    return JSON.stringify(filter_data);
  }

  function get_order_data_json() {     
    var order_data = {
      'value': $('.orderby-label').attr('data-value'),
      'order': $('.orderby-label').attr('data-order')
    }
    return JSON.stringify(order_data);
  }

  function problem_list_filter() {
    $("#filter-loading").show();
    $.ajax({
      url: "/" + window.language_code + "/problem/" +
           "?filter_data=" + get_filter_data_json() +
           "&order_by=" + get_order_data_json(),
      type: "GET",
      success: function(data) {
        $("#problem_list_pagination").html($( data ).find("#problem_list_pagination").html());
        if ($( data ).find(".nextPage").html() != undefined) {
          $(".nextPage").html($( data ).find(".nextPage").html());
          $(".nextPage").attr('href', $( data ).find(".nextPage").attr('href'));
        }
        else
          $(".nextPage").attr('href', '');
        $("#filter-loading").hide();
      }
    });
  }

  $('.filter-option').on('click', function() {
    var category = $(this).attr('category');
    var name = "";
    if (category == 'tag')
      name = $(this).attr('name');
    else
      name = $(this).html();
    var dataValue = $(this).attr('data-value');
    var filterLabel =
        "<span class='text-sm m-l-sm filter-label' " +
        "category='" + category + "' " +
        "data-value='" + dataValue + "' " +
        "id='filter-" + name.replace(/\s/g,"") + "'>" + name +
        "<a href='#' class='m-t-n-sm filter-remove' id-name='" + name.replace(/\s/g,"") + "'> " +
        "<i class='fa fa-times'></i></a>" +
        "</span>";

    if ($('#filter-'+name).length == 0) // This filter label doesn't exists.
      $('#filter-set').append(filterLabel);
    problem_list_filter(); // filter problems by filter label set
  });

  $(document).on('click', '.filter-remove', function() {
    var idName = '#filter-' + $(this).attr("id-name").replace(/\s/g,"");;
    $(idName).remove();
    problem_list_filter();
  });

  $('.orderby-option').on('click', function() {
    var label = $(this).attr('data-label');         
    var value = $(this).attr('data-value');
    var order = $(this).attr('data-order');

    $('.orderby-label').html('<i class="fa fa-sort-numeric-' + order + '"></i> ' + label);
    $('.orderby-label').attr('data-value', value);
    $('.orderby-label').attr('data-order', order);
    problem_list_filter();

    if (order == 'desc') {
        order = 'asc'; 
    } else {
        order = 'desc';
    }
    $(this).attr('data-order', order);
  });

</script>
